## 6. ‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏ü‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Å‡πå‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏ô (Functional Requirements)

> **‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏:** Section ‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÇ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏á‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á IAM-style Functional Requirement Template ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏≠‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏î Context, Edge Case, Workflow, Example ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠

### 6.1 Tier Management

**Description:**  
‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏î‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å (Tier) ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏¢‡∏∑‡∏î‡∏´‡∏¢‡∏∏‡πà‡∏ô ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Dynamic/Fixed/Hybrid Tier ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ä‡∏∏‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Product ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Partner  
‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î Promotion/Demotion Criteria, Lifespan, Grace Period, Priority, Audit Trail ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á

**Key Functions / Features:**

- ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á, ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç, ‡∏•‡∏ö Tier (Dynamic, Fixed, Hybrid)
- ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î Promotion/Demotion Criteria (Transaction, Engagement, Custom Attribute)
- ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î Lifespan, Grace Period, Reset Cycle ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Tier
- ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Multi-Tier Schema (‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å 1 ‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢ Tier ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢ Product ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢ Partner)
- ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î Priority/Weight ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ Tier ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Conflict
- Manual Override ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Tier ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢ Admin
- Audit Trail ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ History Tracking ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á Tier
- ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î Cycle ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥ (‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô/‡∏™‡∏±‡∏õ‡∏î‡∏≤‡∏´‡πå/‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô/‡∏õ‡∏µ)

**Context & Use Case:**  
‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏†‡∏±‡∏ì‡∏ë‡πå‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏û‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ò‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏£ ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ‡∏•‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Gold ‡πÉ‡∏ô Product A ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Silver ‡πÉ‡∏ô Partner X  
‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å IAM/Behavior/Transaction ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞ Tier

**Edge Case / Condition:**  

- Tier conflict ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏´‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á schema (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Gold ‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏á Product ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô)  
- Multi-tenant isolation  
- Tier combination ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö multi-product  
- Tier Lifespan ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏, Grace Period, ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Reset ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥  
- Manual Override ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î Conflict ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö Rule ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥  
- ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Merge User Account ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Split Account  

**Workflow:**  

1. Admin ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Tier ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î Promotion/Demotion Criteria  
2. ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ô Condition ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Event ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Transaction/Behavior  
3. ‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏Ç ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô/‡∏•‡∏î Tier ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å Audit Trail  
4. ‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á Tier ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Notification/Email/In-app  
5. Admin ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ Override Tier ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢ Manual Action ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏ï‡∏∏‡∏ú‡∏•  

**Example:**  
‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏µ Tier Gold ‡πÉ‡∏ô Product A ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Silver ‡πÉ‡∏ô Partner X ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô  
‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å Promote ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Platinum ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á Spend > 50,000 ‡πÉ‡∏ô 3 ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô  
Admin ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Tier ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Gold ‡∏ä‡∏±‡πà‡∏ß‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ß 7 ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏•‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏≤ VIP ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô

### 6.2 Benefit Management

**Description:**  
‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏ä‡∏ô‡πå (Benefit) ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ Tier/Product/Partner ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏¢‡∏∑‡∏î‡∏´‡∏¢‡∏∏‡πà‡∏ô  
‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Benefit ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏†‡∏ó (‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏£/‡∏ä‡∏±‡πà‡∏ß‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ß/‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏Ç), Inheritance, Accumulative, Bundle, Exclusive, Limited User, ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Template

**Key Functions / Features:**

- ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á, ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç, ‡∏•‡∏ö Benefit (Discount, Access, Reward, Partner Benefit)
- ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î Benefit ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ Tier/Product/Partner ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
- ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Benefit Inheritance (Tier ‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Tier ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤)
- ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Benefit ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏†‡∏ó‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ß‡∏£, ‡∏ä‡∏±‡πà‡∏ß‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏ß, ‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏Ç, Bundle, Exclusive, Limited User
- ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Benefit Template ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≥‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÅ‡∏Ñ‡∏°‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏ç
- ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏° Benefit ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢ Tier (Accumulative)
- ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞ Benefit ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö Real-time
- ‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô/‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ Benefit ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ

**Context & Use Case:**  
‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢ Tier ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô Welcome Pack, Anniversary Bonus, Tier Upgrade Gift  
Benefit Inheritance ‡∏ó‡∏≥‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ Tier ‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Tier ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≥‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥

**Edge Case / Condition:**  

- Benefit ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏  
- Benefit ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏à‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°/Event-based  
- Benefit ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏° Partner  
- Benefit ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö Exclusive/Limited User  
- Bundle Benefit (‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô)  
- ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Revoke Benefit ‡∏¢‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ‡∏û‡∏ö Fraud)  

**Workflow:**  

1. Admin ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Benefit Template ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏†‡∏ó‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏Ç  
2. ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏°‡∏≠‡∏ö Benefit ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° Tier/Condition ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Event  
3. ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ Benefit ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ/‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î‡∏≠‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏∏ ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô  
4. ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏î‡∏π Benefit ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö Real-time ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Mobile/Web/Partner App  
5. Admin ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ Revoke/Extend Benefit ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ  

**Example:**  
‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Welcome Pack (‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß), Anniversary Bonus (‡∏õ‡∏µ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á), Tier Upgrade Gift (‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô Tier) ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô  
‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå Exclusive ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ 100 ‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏£‡∏Å  
‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Bundle Benefit (Discount + Free Delivery + Event Access) ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Platinum

### 6.3 Point Policy

**Description:**  
‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏° (Point Policy) ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°, ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ, ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏°  
‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á Rate, Cap, Multiplier ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° Tier/Product/Partner ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Multi-source Aggregation, Priority Rule, Transaction Log

**Key Functions / Features:**

- ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î Point Rate, Cap, Multiplier ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° Tier/Product/Partner
- ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Multi-source Points Aggregation ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Priority Rule
- ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á Policy ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ Product ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Partner ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ
- ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö Transaction Logs ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Audit/Reconciliation
- ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö Loyalty Service ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ Redeem/Convert Points
- ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î Cap ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô/Seasonal, Multiplier ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Event, Policy ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ Partner
- ‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö Real-time ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏¢‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á

**Context & Use Case:**  
‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏°‡∏™‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏ï‡∏Å‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏•‡πà‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏≤ ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô Spend ‡πÉ‡∏ô HR ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ 1x ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏°, Vendor 2x, Partner 3x  
‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏°‡∏û‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏®‡∏©‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° Event ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Cap ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏≤

**Edge Case / Condition:**  

- Daily/Seasonal Cap  
- Multi-source points aggregation  
- Partner-specific multiplier  
- ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡∏±‡∏î‡πÅ‡∏¢‡πâ‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÅ‡∏´‡∏•‡πà‡∏á  
- ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Transaction ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¥‡∏Å/Refund  

**Workflow:**  

1. Admin ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á Point Policy ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ Tier/Product/Partner  
2. ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î Transaction ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ì‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö Real-time ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö Policy  
3. ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö Transaction Log ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö Cap/Multiplier  
4. ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏°‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å Redeem/Convert ‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Loyalty Service ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Partner  
5. ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏ì‡∏µ Transaction ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å Refund ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏°‡∏¢‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô  

**Example:**  
Spend ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö HR ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ 1x ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏°, Spend ‡πÉ‡∏ô Vendor ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ 2x ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏°, Spend ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö Partner ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ 3x ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏°  
‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏°‡∏™‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡∏™‡∏∏‡∏î 5,000 ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏ô, ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ß‡∏á Event ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ Multiplier 2x ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ Tier Gold  
‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Transaction ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å Refund ‡∏à‡∏∞‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏´‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥

### 6.4 Event Management

**Description:**  
‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏´‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Privilege Event ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô Reward Campaign, Birthday Gift, Exclusive Event  
‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏á‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÑ‡∏Ç‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå, Reward Pool, Claim Rule, Trigger/Schedule, Metrics Tracking ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Cross-system Event

**Key Functions / Features:**

- ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á, ‡πÅ‡∏Å‡πâ‡πÑ‡∏Ç, ‡∏•‡∏ö Privilege Event (Birthday Gift, Double Points, Exclusive Party)
- ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î Eligibility Condition, Reward Pool, Claim Rule, Schedule/Trigger Event
- ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Event ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏° Product/Partner (Cross-system Event)
- Reward Pool ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏î, First-come-first-serve, Random Draw
- Metrics Tracking (Engagement Rate, Claim Rate, Conversion Rate)
- ‡∏ï‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á Trigger ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢ (Auto, Manual, Campaign-based)
- Multi-tier/Multi-product Participation Rule
- ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö Eligibility ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏õ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏ï Claim Status ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥

**Context & Use Case:**  
‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏à‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°‡∏û‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏®‡∏©‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ï‡∏∏‡πâ‡∏ô Engagement ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô Weekend Double Points, Birthday Gift, Exclusive Party  
‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Event ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏ú‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö Partner Ecosystem

**Edge Case / Condition:**  

- Event ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏° Tenant  
- Limited-cap Event  
- Duplicate Claim Prevention  
- Event ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ Tier ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Cross-system  
- Event ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¥‡∏Å/‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏á‡∏Ç‡∏ì‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡∏î‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£  

**Workflow:**  

1. Admin ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Event ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î Rule, Reward Pool, Schedule  
2. ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î/‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î Event ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° Trigger/Schedule ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Manual  
3. ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å Claim Reward ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° Eligibility, ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô Duplicate Claim  
4. ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö Track Metrics, Update Dashboard, ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ Reward Pool ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏î  
5. ‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏ì‡∏µ Event ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏¢‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏•‡∏¥‡∏Å ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏∑‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å  

**Example:**  
"Weekend Double Points" ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ Tier Silver ‡πÉ‡∏ô Partner X  
"Birthday Gift" ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏ô‡∏±‡πâ‡∏ô  
"Cross-Partner Challenge" ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà Join Event ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á 2 Platform  

### 6.5 Integration

**Description:**  
‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö IAM, Loyalty Service, Product ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Partner Systems  
‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î API ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ñ‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå, ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Security, Data Consistency, Multi-tenant Integration, Attribute Mapping

**Key Functions / Features:**

- ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ IAM ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏∑‡∏ô‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ï‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Attribute/Identity
- ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ Loyalty Service ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠ Sync ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏°/Reward Transaction ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö Real-time
- ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡∏¥‡∏î API ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Product/Partner ‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏î‡∏π Tier, Benefit, Reward
- ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö OAuth2, Webhook, Event Bus ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Integration ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ä‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏≤‡∏á
- ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Edge Case ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô Network Failure, Retry Logic, Data Consistency, Multi-tenant Isolation
- Mapping Attribute ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ Partner ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Validation Rule ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞
- Security & Data Privacy ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô

**Context & Use Case:**  
Privilege Service ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô‡∏®‡∏π‡∏ô‡∏¢‡πå‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö IAM, Loyalty, Partner  
‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Multi-tenant, Cross-Platform, Federated Privilege Validation

**Edge Case / Condition:**  

- Network failure, Retry logic  
- Data inconsistency, Out-of-order event  
- Attribute Mapping ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏á, Validation Rule ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ Partner  
- Multi-tenant Isolation  
- Security Breach, Data Privacy Violation  

**Workflow:**  

1. ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Event/Request ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å IAM, Loyalty, Product, Partner  
2. ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö Security, Attribute, Data Consistency, Validation Rule  
3. Sync ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• Privilege ‡πÑ‡∏õ‡∏¢‡∏±‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö Real-time ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Batch  
4. ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î/Retry ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥, Logging, Alerting  
5. ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö Compliance (GDPR/PDPA) ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Export/Share ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•  

**Example:**  
‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏°‡∏±‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Partner ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Tier/Benefit ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö Privilege  
‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏°‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏•‡πÉ‡∏ô Partner B ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏™‡∏ñ‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏°‡∏•‡∏î‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö  
‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Partner ‡∏™‡πà‡∏á Webhook ‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á Transaction, ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö Privilege Sync ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Benefit ‡∏ó‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ

### 6.6 Analytics & Personalization

**Description:**  
‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡∏û‡∏§‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Recommendation, Dashboard, KPI, Trend Analysis  
‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö ML/AI Engine ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Personalized Privilege, Scenario Simulation, Predictive Analytics

**Key Functions / Features:**

- ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö Usage Pattern ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏à‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏£‡∏° Reward
- ML/AI Recommendation Engine ‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥ Benefit, Tier, ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Reward ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°
- Dashboard ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Business User ‡∏î‡∏π Tier Distribution, Benefit Utilization, KPI, Trend
- ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° KPI ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Trend Analysis ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏î‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏à‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏ó‡∏ò‡πå
- ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Data Lag, Missing Attribute, Inconsistent Event Logs
- ‡∏ô‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Campaign ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö Personalized

**Context & Use Case:**  
‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° Engagement, Upsell, Cross-sell, ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏ó‡∏ò‡πå, Personalized Reward  
Admin ‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏•‡∏∂‡∏Å‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å Dashboard, ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏≥‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥ Reward ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°

**Edge Case / Condition:**  

- Data lag  
- Missing attribute  
- Inconsistent event logs  
- KPI Calculation Error  
- Data Privacy Compliance (GDPR/PDPA)  

**Workflow:**  

1. ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏° Usage Pattern ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• Reward ‡πÅ‡∏ö‡∏ö Real-time/Batch  
2. ML/AI ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡∏û‡∏§‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥ Benefit/Tier ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Predict Churn  
3. Admin ‡∏î‡∏π Dashboard, Export/Share Report, Drill-down ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢ Tier/Benefit/Event  
4. ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏™‡πà‡∏á Personalized Campaign ‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏ú‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô Notification/Email  
5. ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö Data Privacy Compliance ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô Export/Share  

**Example:**  
‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏ô‡∏≥ Upgrade Tier ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Reward ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ß‡πÇ‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á  
‡∏î‡∏π‡∏™‡∏±‡∏î‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ Tier, Utilization Rate ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ Benefit  
‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Predict ‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡πÑ‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏µ‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ß‡πÇ‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏° Churn ‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏≠ Campaign ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏®‡∏©

### 6.7 Data-driven Evolution

**Description:**  
‡∏Ç‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö Privilege ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏¢‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏¢‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏°‡πå  
‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Historical Analysis, Real-time Adjustment, Predictive Modeling, Scenario Simulation, Fraud Detection

**Key Functions / Features:**

- ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏¢‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á (Historical Data Analysis)
- ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Tier/Benefit/Event/Point Policy ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• Real-time ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Predictive Model
- ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á Scenario (Simulation) ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏ó‡∏ò‡πå‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏ö
- ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Outlier User Behavior, Fraud Detection, Partner-specific Anomaly
- Adaptive Policy suggestion based on historical & real-time data
- Dashboard ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Scenario Simulation ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Strategic Planning

**Context & Use Case:**  
‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ú‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏ó‡∏ò‡πå, ‡∏ó‡∏î‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Policy ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà, ‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏à‡∏±‡∏ö Fraud, ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Policy ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥  
Admin ‡πÄ‡∏´‡πá‡∏ô‡∏ú‡∏• Simulation ‡∏Å‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏à‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏á

**Edge Case / Condition:**  

- Outlier user behavior  
- Fraud detection  
- Partner-specific anomaly  
- Data retention, GDPR/PDPA Compliance  
- Data Drift ‡πÉ‡∏ô Predictive Model  

**Workflow:**  

1. ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏Å‡πá‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏¢‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ô‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏£‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏•‡πÑ‡∏ó‡∏°‡πå  
2. Admin ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Scenario, ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏ö ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏•‡πÉ‡∏ô Dashboard  
3. ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Policy ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏û‡∏ö Pattern ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô Admin  
4. Export/Share ‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏∞‡∏´‡πå ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° Mask ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏•‡∏™‡πà‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏ö‡∏∏‡∏Ñ‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° Compliance  

**Example:**  
‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° Point Rate ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏î‡∏π‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏ö‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ Reward Utilization  
‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏à‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏û‡∏§‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏£‡∏° Fraud ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå ‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Claim Reward ‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≥ ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Benefit ‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏õ‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏¥  
‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Policy ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏û‡∏ö Outlier ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ß‡πÇ‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏°‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà

### 6.8 Multi-Tier / Multi-Product / Multi-Partner Support

**Description:**  
‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å 1 ‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢ Tier ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢ Product/Partner ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô  
‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Schema, Rule, Policy, Conflict, Priority, Multi-tenant Isolation, Attribute Mapping ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö

**Key Functions / Features:**

- ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å 1 ‡∏Ñ‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏π‡πà‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢ Tier ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢ Product/Partner ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô
- ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î Schema, Rule, Policy ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ Product/Partner
- ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Conflict, Priority, ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Combination ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á Tier/Benefit ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏° Product/Partner
- ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Multi-tenant Isolation ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Attribute Mapping ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ Product/Partner
- ‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Tier Schema ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤ Product/Partner ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà
- ‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏° Benefit/Privilege ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å Tier/Product/Partner (Accumulative ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Exclusive ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° Policy)

**Context & Use Case:**  
‡∏ò‡∏∏‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏à‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ú‡∏•‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏†‡∏±‡∏ì‡∏ë‡πå‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏û‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ò‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏£ ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Privilege ‡πÅ‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏®‡∏π‡∏ô‡∏¢‡πå  
‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Platinum ‡πÉ‡∏ô Product B ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Bronze ‡πÉ‡∏ô Partner Y ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô

**Edge Case / Condition:**  

- Tier Conflict (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Gold ‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏á Product ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô)  
- Multi-Tenant Isolation  
- Attribute Mapping ‡πÄ‡∏â‡∏û‡∏≤‡∏∞ Partner  
- ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Merge/Split User Account  

**Workflow:**  

1. ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤ Product/Partner ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á Tier Schema ‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥  
2. ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏° Benefit/Privilege ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å Tier/Product/Partner ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° Policy (Accumulative ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Exclusive)  
3. ‡∏à‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£ Conflict/Priority ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥ ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° Logging  
4. Admin ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ Override ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Merge Benefit ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏ì‡∏µ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πÄ‡∏®‡∏©  

**Example:**  
‡∏•‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Platinum ‡πÉ‡∏ô Product B, Bronze ‡πÉ‡∏ô Partner Y ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô  
‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå‡∏™‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å Product/Partner ‡πÉ‡∏ô Ecosystem ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô  
‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Merge Account ‡πÅ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå/Benefit ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏ä‡∏µ‡∏ñ‡∏π‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° Policy

## 7. ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏ì‡∏∞ (Non-Functional Requirements)

‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö Privilege ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Ñ‡∏∏‡∏ì‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏ì‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç‡πÉ‡∏ô 8 ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏ô ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ò‡∏∏‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏à‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏∏‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏∏‡πÑ‡∏ß‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ô Section 1 (Purpose) ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Section 3 (Business Requirements)

### 7.1 Performance (‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏û)

- **Response Time:** API ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å (Tier, Benefit, Point, Event) ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏ï‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏™‡∏ô‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô 1 ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ ‡πÉ‡∏ô 95% ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏ì‡∏µ
- **Throughput:** ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Concurrent Requests ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢ 1,000 ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£/‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ (Scalable)
- **Event Latency:** ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏ß‡∏•‡∏ú‡∏• Event ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏ô 5 ‡∏ß‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ (P95) ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Real-time Event
- **Batch Processing:** Batch Job (Tier Evaluation, Point Aggregation, Data Export) ‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏£‡πá‡∏à‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô SLA ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î (‡πÄ‡∏ä‡πà‡∏ô 95% ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô 30 ‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ)

### 7.2 Scalability (‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Ç‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏¢)

- **Architecture:** ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô Microservice ‡∏™‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ñ Scale-out ‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ Service ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¥‡∏™‡∏£‡∏∞ (Stateless/Stateful)
- **Horizontal Scaling:** ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏°‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏¥‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ì Transaction ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Peak Load
- **Multi-Tenant:** ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Multi-Tenant, Multi-Product, Multi-Partner ‡πÇ‡∏î‡∏¢‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ó‡∏ö Performance ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏µ Isolation

### 7.3 Security (‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏õ‡∏•‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏†‡∏±‡∏¢)

- **Authentication/Authorization:** ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö OAuth2, JWT, RBAC, API Key
- **Data Encryption:** ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á In-Transit (TLS 1.2+) ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ At-Rest (AES-256 ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡πÄ‡∏ó‡πà‡∏≤)
- **Audit & Monitoring:** ‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∂‡∏Å Audit Log ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡∏∏‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏à‡∏Å‡∏£‡∏£‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç ‡∏û‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏° Monitoring, Alert, ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Export
- **Data Privacy:** ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö GDPR/PDPA, Consent Management, Data Minimization, Data Masking

### 7.4 Reliability (‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ô‡πà‡∏≤‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏ñ‡∏∑‡∏≠)

- **Uptime:** Uptime ‡πÑ‡∏°‡πà‡∏ô‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡∏Å‡∏ß‡πà‡∏≤ 99.9% ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô
- **High Availability:** ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö HA, DR Plan ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Failover ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô 5 ‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ó‡∏µ
- **Fault Tolerance:** ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Retry, Circuit Breaker, Graceful Degradation ‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏õ‡∏±‡∏ç‡∏´‡∏≤
- **Data Consistency:** ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏π‡∏• Privilege, Loyalty, Partner ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á Consistent ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å Integration, ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Eventual Consistency/Bulk Reconciliation

### 7.5 Maintainability (‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏î‡∏π‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏£‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏©‡∏≤)

- **Code Structure:** Modular/Layered Architecture, Separation of Concerns, Code Review
- **Automated Testing:** ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡∏∏‡∏° Unit, Integration, E2E Test, Regression Test
- **CI/CD:** Pipeline ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Deploy/Release ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡πÇ‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥, Rollback, Canary Deployment
- **Documentation:** ‡∏°‡∏µ API Spec, Integration Guide, User Manual ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏ô, Version Control
- **Logging/Monitoring:** ‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å Service ‡∏°‡∏µ Logging, Monitoring, Alerting, Trace ID

### 7.6 Usability (‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢)

- **Admin Dashboard:** UX/UI ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢, ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Workflow ‡∏´‡∏•‡∏±‡∏Å‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏ô, Customizable Dashboard
- **API Documentation:** ‡∏ä‡∏±‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏à‡∏ô, ‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô, ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡∏∏‡∏° Use Case ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ç, Interactive API Playground
- **Multi-language:** ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏´‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏©‡∏≤ (‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏à‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πá‡∏ô) ‡∏ó‡∏±‡πâ‡∏á UI ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Content
- **Error Message & Help:** ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏ú‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏û‡∏•‡∏≤‡∏î‡πÄ‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏à‡∏á‡πà‡∏≤‡∏¢, ‡∏°‡∏µ Help/Support, Knowledge Base

### 7.7 Compliance (‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏õ‡∏è‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏±‡∏ö)

- **Data Retention:** ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏ô‡πÇ‡∏¢‡∏ö‡∏≤‡∏¢ Data Retention, Export, Deletion ‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Å‡∏é‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢ (Configurable Policy)
- **Consent Management:** ‡∏°‡∏µ Mechanism ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Consent, Data Subject Rights (DSR), Consent Audit Trail
- **Standard Compliance:** ‡∏õ‡∏è‡∏¥‡∏ö‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° ISO 27001, GDPR, PDPA ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ê‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏µ‡πà‡∏¢‡∏ß‡∏Ç‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á, ‡∏£‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö External Audit

### 7.8 Observability & Monitoring (‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏±‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏ï‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ì‡πå‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏ß‡∏à‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏ö)

- **Real-time Monitoring:** ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏° Health, Performance, Error Rate ‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏•‡∏∞ Service, Dashboard Real-time
- **Alerting:** ‡πÅ‡∏à‡πâ‡∏á‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏¥‡∏î Incident, SLA Breach, ‡∏´‡∏£‡∏∑‡∏≠ Security Event, Custom Alert Rule
- **Audit Trail:** Export Audit Log ‡∏™‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö Compliance ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Investigation, Search/Filter/Drill-down

---

## 8. ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏ì‡∏ë‡πå‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ä‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏î (Success Criteria & KPIs)

‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡πâ‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∞‡πÄ‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ô‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö Privilege ‡πÑ‡∏î‡πâ‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏ó‡∏∏‡∏Å‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏¥ ‡∏Å‡∏≥‡∏´‡∏ô‡∏î Success Criteria ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ KPIs ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡∏™‡∏≠‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏•‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö Business Value (Section 4), Functional/Non-functional Requirements (Section 6,7) ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Scope (Section 2)

### 8.1 Strategic Success Criteria

| ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏á‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏¢‡∏∏‡∏ó‡∏ò‡πå (Strategic Goal) | ‡πÄ‡∏Å‡∏ì‡∏ë‡πå‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏î‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏™‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏£‡πá‡∏à (Success Criteria)                         |
| -------------------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------- |
| ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏¥‡πà‡∏° Engagement ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Loyalty    | ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏°‡∏≤‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ã‡πâ‡∏≥ (Retention Rate) ‚â• 30% ‡∏†‡∏≤‡∏¢‡πÉ‡∏ô 6 ‡πÄ‡∏î‡∏∑‡∏≠‡∏ô‡πÅ‡∏£‡∏Å |
| ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏ï‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å Tier ‡∏™‡∏π‡∏á         | ‡∏≠‡∏±‡∏ï‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡πÄ‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏ö‡πÇ‡∏ï‡∏Ç‡∏≠‡∏á‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ä‡∏¥‡∏Å Tier Gold/Platinum ‚â• 10% ‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏µ         |
| ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏Ç‡∏¢‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏û‡∏±‡∏ô‡∏ò‡∏°‡∏¥‡∏ï‡∏£‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Ecosystem       | ‡∏à‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏ß‡∏ô Partner ‡∏ó‡∏µ‡πà‡πÄ‡∏ä‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏°‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏´‡∏°‡πà ‚â• 3 ‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢/‡∏õ‡∏µ                         |
| ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏™‡∏£‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏û‡∏∂‡∏á‡∏û‡∏≠‡πÉ‡∏à‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡∏™‡∏¥‡∏ó‡∏ò‡∏¥‡πå           | ‡∏Ñ‡∏∞‡πÅ‡∏ô‡∏ô NPS ‚â• 60 ‡∏à‡∏≤‡∏Å‡∏Å‡∏•‡∏∏‡πà‡∏°‡∏ú‡∏π‡πâ‡πÉ‡∏ä‡πâ Privilege                        |

### 8.2 Operational KPIs

| ‡∏´‡∏°‡∏ß‡∏î (Category)    | ‡∏ï‡∏±‡∏ß‡∏ä‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏±‡∏î (KPI)                            | ‡πÄ‡∏õ‡πâ‡∏≤‡∏´‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏¢ (Target) |

KPIs ‡πÄ‡∏´‡∏•‡πà‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏µ‡πâ‡∏ï‡πâ‡∏≠‡∏á‡πÅ‡∏™‡∏î‡∏á‡∏ú‡∏•‡πÉ‡∏ô Dashboard ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏°‡∏µ‡∏Å‡∏≤‡∏£‡∏ï‡∏¥‡∏î‡∏ï‡∏≤‡∏°/‡∏£‡∏≤‡∏¢‡∏á‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠ Stakeholder ‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏™‡∏°‡πà‡∏≥‡πÄ‡∏™‡∏°‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏±‡∏ö‡∏õ‡∏£‡∏∏‡∏á‡∏£‡∏∞‡∏ö‡∏ö‡∏≠‡∏¢‡πà‡∏≤‡∏á‡∏ï‡πà‡∏≠‡πÄ‡∏ô‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏á ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏£ cross-reference ‡∏Å‡∏±‡∏ö Business Requirements (Section 3) ‡πÅ‡∏•‡∏∞ Non-Functional Requirements (Section 7) ‡πÄ‡∏û‡∏∑‡πà‡∏≠‡∏Ñ‡∏ß‡∏≤‡∏°‡∏Ñ‡∏£‡∏ö‡∏ñ‡πâ‡∏ß‡∏ô
